				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Nimm von uns, Herr, du treuer Gott, BWV 101 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>7 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1724, rev. 1724, after 1735 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>

<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Nimm von uns, Herr, du treuer Gott
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Take from us, Lord, You faithful God
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="ca">Nimm von uns</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>

<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 101&#160;; BC A 118
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 410
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>D minor
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>7 movements:
<ol><li>Choral: Nimm von uns, Herr, du treuer Gott (D&#160;minor)
</li><li>Aria (tenor): Handle nicht nach deinen Rechten (G&#160;minor)
</li><li>Recitativo (soprano): Ach! Herr Gott, durch die Treue dein (D&#160;minor)
</li><li>Aria (bass): Warum willst du so zornig sein? (A&#160;minor)
</li><li>Recitativo (Tenor): Die Sünd hat uns verderbet sehr (D&#160;minor)
</li><li>Aria (soprano, alto): Gedenk an Jesu bittern Tod! (D&#160;minor)
</li><li>Chorale: Leit uns mit deiner rechten Hand (D&#160;minor)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1724, rev. 1724, after 1735 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
